subscribe (sab'iskaraayb) v. -scribed, -scribing. 1 ru kumad; ku-helid joogto, wargays joogto loo helo. e.g. I subscribed to several magazines. 2 ku-deeqid; ku tabarucid. e.g. He subscribed generously to the new mosque. She subscribed $500 to the orphans. 3 sub scribe to, ayidid; ku-raacid fikrad ama aragti; taagyeerid. e.g. I don't prefer to subscribe to anything unfair. 4 ballan-qaadid bixin lacag. 5 joogto-u-bixin rukumad jariirad. 6 ka-qaadatin caddad buug aan wali soo bixin. e.g. The first print has been subscribed. 7 saxiixid; ku-duugid qalid, siiba heshiis, qandaraas, ama marag ahaan. e.g. She subscribe the affidavit as a wit ness. -subscriber n.

tear1(ter) v. tore (toor), torn (toorn), tearing. 1 jeexid ama jeex-jeexid; dillaacin. e.g. She tore the letter in half. I tore up the paper. 2 furid. e.g. He tore open the pack age. 3 daloolin. e.g. The nail tore her skirt. The bullet tore a hole in the door. 4 daloolmid. e.g. Tore his shirt on a nail. 5 be torn between, mid-dooratin ama ukala qaarmid laba. e.g. She was torn between her husband and her family. 6 tarraarid; qar-jeexid; dardarid. e.g. When the bomb exploded, the neighbors tore out of their

homes.

–n. jeex; dalool. e.g. They will sew the tear in your shirt. You have a small tear in your skirt.

–tear one's hair out, [informal] qof ay ka-taal oo jafaaliya timihiis.

–tear someone/something to shreds(or pieces), [informal] rifid ama canaanatin qof.

–tear someone/something apart, a dhambalid, siiba xiriir ka dhexeeya dad. e.g. The bloody civil war had torn our nation apart. b baarid ama qalaaba-gaddin meel.

–tear oneself away, ka-tagid ama go'id wax aad loo rabo. e.g. Many Somalis couldn't tear themselves away from Somalia.

–tear someone/something down, a burburin ama diir-diirid dhisme. b [informal] eedayn ama ciqaabid qof.

–tear into, ku-weerarid hadal qof. –tearable adj.; –tearer n.

–v. ilmayn. e.g. The heavy smoke made her eyes tear. – tearlike adj.

tear gas n. neef sun ah oo indhaha u gaysata cun-cun iyo xanuun ka-ilmeeya.

–v. tear-gas [usu be tear-gassed] ku-furid sun ka-ilmaysa indhaha.
